[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Access Pattern**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The write begins at address [0m[1;36m0x7f893973b528[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This exceeds the [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer capacity by [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Layout**: The shadow byte analysis shows:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `f1` markers indicate stack left redzone[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;36m00[0m[39m` indicates addressable memory[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `f3` markers indicate stack right redzone[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow writes into the right redzone area marked as `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mf3[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Input**: The test case that triggered the issue consists of [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m bytes of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata, starting with the byte sequence `[0m[1;36m0x5b[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x13[0m[33m...[0m[39m`[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following code [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mareas should be examined:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Location**: [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-openvpn.c[0m[39m`, specifically:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Line [0m[1;36m185[0m[39m: Declaration and size of the [0m[32m'buf'[0m[39m variable[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Line [0m[1;36m312[0m[39m: The `tvb_memcpy` call that triggers the overflow[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - The entire `dissect_openvpn_msg_common` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstarting at line [0m[1;36m174[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Copy Operation**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/[0m[95mtvbuff.c[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m945[0m[39m: Implementation of `tvb_memcpy`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the length parameter is calculated and passed to `tvb_memcpy`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **OpenVPN Protocol Handling**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the OpenVPN dissector parses packet headers[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Length field extraction and validation from OpenVPN packets[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any assumptions made about maximum field sizes[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Buffer Size Determination**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Why the [0m[32m'buf'[0m[39m buffer is sized at [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether this size is based on protocol specifications[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If there are conditional paths that could result in larger data being copied[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability appears to be related to insufficient bounds checking when [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopying data from the packet buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m into the fixed-size stack buffer, where [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe source data size exceeds the destination buffer capacity.[0m                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I have identified the root[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability in the OpenVPN dissector. The [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue occurs in the `dissect_openvpn_msg_common` function where:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m185[0m[39m**: An [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte stack buffer `buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` is declared[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m310[0m[39m**: `wkc_len` is read from the packet [0m[1;39m([0m[39mattacker-controlled, [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-bit [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m311[0m[39m**: `data_len = msg_length_remaining - wkc_len` is calculated without [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m312[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, buf, offset, data_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` copies `data_len` bytes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m313[0m[39m**: `strcmp` checks if the data starts with [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer triggered an [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m-byte write into an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer, causing a [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow into the stack's right redzone.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Core Insights[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **The buffer is unnecessary**: The sole purpose is to check if data at `offset` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstarts with [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m string [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m characters[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No validation exists**: There's no check that `data_len > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` or `data_len <= [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m`[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Wireshark provides safe alternatives**: The `[0m[1;35mtvb_strneql[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` function performs [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring comparison directly on tvb data without intermediate buffers[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Pattern established in codebase**: Multiple dissectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-assa_r3.c, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket-beep.c, packet-ath.c, packet-imf.c, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m use `tvb_strneql` for this exact [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse case[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Replace Vulnerable Code with tvb_strneql[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-openvpn.c`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Remove the vulnerable buffer declaration at line [0m[1;36m185[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete: `uint8_t buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This buffer is only used in the vulnerable code block and can be completely [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminated[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Replace the vulnerable code block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m307[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m315[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with safe string [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomparison[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Current code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m307[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m315[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```c[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mopenvpn_opcode == P_CONTROL_HARD_RESET_CLIENT_V3 || openvpn_opcode == [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mP_CONTROL_WKC_V1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      &&  msg_length_remaining >= [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    wkc_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ntohs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    data_len = msg_length_remaining - wkc_len;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, buf, offset, data_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mstrcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m&buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace with:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```c[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mopenvpn_opcode == P_CONTROL_HARD_RESET_CLIENT_V3 || openvpn_opcode == [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mP_CONTROL_WKC_V1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      &&  msg_length_remaining >= [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    wkc_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ntohs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    data_len = msg_length_remaining - wkc_len;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Validate that data_len is reasonable and check for [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m magic string *[0m[35m/[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata_len < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m || [0m[1;35mtvb_strneql[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m7[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix Works[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates the vulnerability**: No intermediate buffer means no buffer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow possible[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Uses safe Wireshark API**: `[0m[1;35mtvb_strneql[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` handles all bounds checking [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternally via `[0m[1;35mensure_contiguous_no_exception[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves exact logic**: The function still checks if data at `offset` starts [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m and returns [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m if it doesn't match[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Handles edge cases**: [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returns [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39minterpreted as != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m if insufficient data exists in tvb[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returns [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m if string doesn't match[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returns [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m if string matches exactly[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Validates data_len**: The check `data_len < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m` prevents negative values [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhen [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwkc_len > msg_length_remaining[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and ensures minimum data for [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m string[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Defense in Depth[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix includes validation that `data_len >= [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m` before calling `tvb_strneql`:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents negative data_len [0m[1;39m([0m[39minteger underflow when wkc_len > [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmsg_length_remaining[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Ensures minimum length for [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m comparison [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Follows Wireshark patterns for minimum length validation seen in packet-bt-dht.c,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket-ifcp.c, etc.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Stack-buffer-overflow**: Eliminated by removing the buffer entirely[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Attacker-controlled length**: `tvb_strneql` safely handles any length via [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternal bounds checking[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fuzzer crash**: The fuzzer input [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m11[0m[39m-byte copy into [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will no [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger trigger overflow[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Protocol correctness**: Wrapped client key packets without [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m magic [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring are still properly rejected[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Same conditional check**: Still only applies to P_CONTROL_HARD_RESET_CLIENT_V3[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand P_CONTROL_WKC_V1 opcodes[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Same validation requirement**: msg_length_remaining >= [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m check preserved[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Same wkc_len extraction**: Line [0m[1;36m310[0m[39m unchanged[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Same data_len calculation**: Line [0m[1;36m311[0m[39m unchanged[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Same early return**: Still returns [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m when [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m string doesn't match[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Downstream code unaffected**: Lines [0m[1;36m317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m338[0m[39m use data_len and wkc_len which are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill calculated the same way[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### No Side Effects[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **No harness modification**: The fix only modifies the dissector logic, not the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing entry points[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No test breakage**: The fix preserves the exact same packet validation logic[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No utility function changes**: Uses existing `tvb_strneql` which is stable and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwidely used[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No external dependency changes**: All changes are within packet-openvpn.c[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No broader codebase impact**: The buf variable is local to this function and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot used elsewhere[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix follows the established pattern used in:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `packet-assa_r3.[0m[1;92mc:6590[0m[39m`: `[0m[1;35mtvb_strneql[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[32m"~~~ds"[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `packet-ath.[0m[1;92mc:75[0m[39m`: `[0m[1;35mtvb_strneql[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[32m"TRIBES-B"[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `packet-pgsql.[0m[1;92mc:272[0m[39m`: `[0m[1;35mtvb_strneql[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnext_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[32m"NTLMSSP"[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m7[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `packet-fix.[0m[1;92mc:167[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m182[0m[39m`: Multiple uses for protocol tag validation[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll these dissectors use `tvb_strneql` for magic string validation without [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintermediate buffers, which is the recommended approach in Wireshark development.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
